NAME: Memory Pizza
ADDR: 
TEXT: ★★★☆☆ 03 Jul 2019 P459+W8Q, Châu Phú A, Châu Đốc, An Giang, Vietnam This comfy western style café is an air con oasis in Chau Doc's busy centre. Prices are reasonable, I just wished the cappuccino was good, sadly it's not, so better to stick with Vietnamese coffee Quán Mekong ★★★★☆ 04 Jul 2019 41 Đ. Lê Lợi, Châu Phú B, Châu Đốc, An Giang, Vietnam I have been visiting this place every time I'm in Chau Doc for almost fifteen years now. It has a brilliant location inside a quiet courtyard in front of an old, dilapidated colonial villa, and if it wasn't for the small plastic chairs and tables, this could be a romantic, upmarket dining spot. As it is, though, it's just a basic local eatery, but that's not a bad thing. I never had a bad meal here, actually. They have an English menu and cater to tourists as well, so you pay a little bit more than in other basic street eateries, but the food is still inexpensive by any standards and I like the atmosphere here. Quán Phở Dũng ★★★★☆ 03 Jul 2019 263 Nguyễn Văn Thoại, Châu Phú A, Châu Đốc, An Giang, Vietnam This is the place to come when a proper bowl of phở is what you are after in Châu Đốc. Nothing fancy, just a simple local eatery serving excellent, deeply satisfying soups at very fair prices. A large bowl for 30k is hard to argue with.

PROV: Bà Rịa – Vũng Tàu / Côn Đảo
NAME: Beach House Restaurant & Cocktails Côn Đảo
ADDR: 
TEXT: ★★★★★ 03 Jan 2023 · ₫100–200k · Dinner Phan Chu Trinh, khu 2, island, Bà Rịa - Vũng Tàu 790000, Vietnam We stayed just next door so this became our go to restaurant during our time in Con Dao. But it's well worth a visit no matter where you're staying as Beach House is certainly one of the best restaurants on the island. It's run by a young couple and has a surprisingly international menu of home-cooked, mostly healthy dishes from squid tagliatelle to a delicious vegan naan sandwich. Prices are really good and there's cold beer for 20k. Highly recommended CocoDeli Kem Dừa Côn Đảo ★★★★★ 14 May 2022 Khu 9 Nguyễn Văn Cừ, Côn Đảo, Bà Rịa - Vũng Tàu, Vietnam This is another one dish only ice cream shop, new and less famous than the one up the road where all the tourist cars stop. The one dish they sell is Coconut ice cream, an island specialty, and as delicious as it sounds. What I don't understand though : this place has the most wonderful location in a large shady palm grove and yet there's no beverages, no coffee, no beers, it feels like such a waste of prime space. Price here is 60k for a cup, more expensive than up the road for the same quality and quantity, but if atmosphere is more important than price, I'd recommend coming here. Coconut ice cream stall ★★★★★ 13 May 2022 Only one dish available here, not even coffee. Delicious coconut ice cream, served in half a coconut with fresh coconut juice on the side. It's 40k for a fairly large portion of creamy bliss. It seems to be a Con Dao specialty and definitely worth sinning for. Infiniti Cafe & Restaurant ★★★★★ 20 May 2026 Khu 8 Đ. Trần Phú, Côn Đảo, Hồ Chí Minh, Vietnam Infiniti is hands down the island's nicest place for a good coffee, with its chic modern décor, air conditioning, and good Wi-Fi. There's a rather pricey menu of international dishes, but we only ever came here for coffee. In fact, this became our daily coffee stop because it's the best place in town for that. They do very nice Vietnamese-style coffees, including cà phê dừa, or coconut coffee, as well as pretty decent espresso drinks. The Secret Restaurant ★★★★★ 20 May 2026 Đặc Khu, 08 Tôn Đức Thắng, Côn Đảo, Hồ Chí Minh 790000, Vietnam The Secret Restaurant is part of one of Con Dao's fancier hotels along the promenade, and its terrace offers beautiful views over the deep blue sea and the sweeping bay. The menu features a fairly extensive range of international dishes, from dim sum to pizza, alongside more traditional Vietnamese fare. Food prices won't break the bank, although the drinks are quite expensive, which is fair enough given the luxurious setting. It's also one of the very few places in Vietnam where we were treated to an amuse-gueule, in this case baguette with pâté, which was a nice touch. Worth coming here just to enjoy the atmosphere, even if it's only for coffee and cake. Gia Minh Hand-made Noodle Bistro ★★★★★ 20 May 2026 Đường Lương Thế Trân, Quần Đảo, Côn Đảo, Hồ Chí Minh 78800, Vietnam This is a very basic-looking eatery, albeit in a pleasant garden setting. But appearances can be deceptive. The food here is outstanding, especially anything featuring their handmade noodles. The wonton noodle soup is delicious, and the grilled squid served on a bed of noodles is equally good. They also do very good spring rolls and salads, so this is an absolute must for anyone visiting the islands. Prices are reasonable as well.

Cô Ba Restaurant ★★★★★ 02 Jun 2026 1 Hoàng Hoa Thám, Vũng Tàu, Hồ Chí Minh 790000, Vietnam This is probably Vũng Tàu’s most popular eatery, a large, busy place specialising in the regional specialty bánh khọt, the number one local dish, but also offering other options such as bánh xèo and com tam. It’s better than some of the reviews suggest. As a matter of fact, I really enjoyed the food here a lot. Prices are good, too. Gành Hào 2 Seafood Restaurant ★★★★☆ 02 Jun 2026 83QC+RM3, 09 Hạ Long, Thành phố Vũng Tầu, Bà Rịa - Vũng Tàu, Vietnam This is a massive seafood restaurant right by the sea, next to the jetty where the fast boats leave for Con Dao. And where else would you want to be while waiting for the ferry, enjoying sea views and good food? It’s not a budget place, obviously, but prices are reasonable, as you would expect in a spot mainly frequented by domestic tourists and locals. Cask Bar ★★★★★ 02 Jun 2026 Front Beach, 12 Quang Trung, Vũng Tàu, Hồ Chí Minh, Vietnam Cask Bar has a large selection of Vietnamese craft beers in bottles, and even the best of them, Pasteur Street, on tap. Their happy hour coincides with sunset, so sitting on the west-facing balcony with sea views and enjoying a sundowner beer is highly recommended, and should definitely be on your bucket list of things to do in Vung Tau. CARIBAN COFFEE ★★★★★ 02 Jun 2026 126D Hoàng Hoa Thám, Vũng Tàu, Hồ Chí Minh 78207, Vietnam If you're looking for a perfectly prepared flat white made with quality beans, served in a beautifully decorated coffee shop with cool air conditioning, look no further than Cariban. It's the only place you'll need in Vung Tau to satisfy those cravings. A welcome refuge from the heat, and at 60k, very reasonably priced. Bánh Khọt cây Sung ★★★★☆ 02 Jun 2026 19 Hoàng Hoa Thám, Vũng Tàu, Hồ Chí Minh, Vietnam A basic local eatery that specialises in one dish, the regional specialty called bánh khọt—small deep-fried rice flour cakes, served with seafood or meat toppings of your choice. This is not health food, but it’s cheap and very tasty, and it comes with plenty of fresh leaves and pickles, which makes it feel slightly lighter than it is. Bắc Giang Nhà nghỉ Đương Soài ★★☆☆☆ 26 Jun 2020 5QHG+FC2, Thôn Đồng Rì , tt. Thanh Sơn H, Sơn Động, Bắc Giang 26427, Vietnam The girl running this place is very nice and speaks good English, but it's a run down, eerie place in a remote industrial wasteland where you'd only want to spend the night if you have absolutely no other option. 200k for a room that hasn't been refurbished since around 1998 Bắc Kạn Café sân vườn 279 ★★★★★ 29 Jun 2020 CPX9+GP9, TT. Chợ Rầm, Ba Bể, Bắc Kạn, Vietnam If we were anywhere south of the Northern mountain area, I wouldn't even review this place, let alone give five stars. It's pretty much your standard Vietnamese garden café of which there are usually dozens in most towns, and generally at least a couple in most villages in the south. In this area, however, this place is an oasis in the desert. Not only are there hardly any cafés at all within 50 kilometres, this one even serves real, good quality Daklak coffee by filter at a low price (20k with or without milk and ice). Plus, it's friendly, there's plugs, sofas and WiFi. Nhà Hàng Văn Khoa 2 ★★★☆☆ 07 Jul 2020 Bố Lù, Ba Bể District, Bắc Kạn, Vietnam We ended up having lunch here simply because is was the only place that was open on a Monday during Covid19. It's a large restaurant that seems to cater mostly to bigger groups but we were the only guests. No menu was available, but they cooked us some fried rice, fries and the local lap suon sausage. The food was alright but nothing special and rather pricy. We paid 180k for the three dishes and 2 beers. But without competition, oh well... Nice views Ba Be Lake View Homestay ★★★★☆ 07 Jul 2020 Ba Be National Park Tour, Pac Ngoi, Ba Bể, Bắc Kạn, Vietnam The small rooms (180k) are quite basic as is expected of a homestay, but they have ac and hot water. The views from the upstairs terrace are quite wonderful, their home cooked food (around 100k/pax) is generous and plentiful but a bit on the safe side and bland. Ba Bể National Park ★★★★☆ 06 Mar 2024 Bố Lù, Ba Bể District, Bắc Kạn 23511, Vietnam Ba Be is a surprisingly low key tourist destination, a picture perfect mountain lake surrounded by gorgeous scenery. The main accommodation options are simple homestays in a small hilltribe village. It's a lovely place, but sadly, while the lake is nice to look at, there's not much to do, really. Boat trips are more geared towards domestic tour groups and quite pricey, and I didn't find any suitable place for a nice swim anywhere around.

Prices are very reasonable and they also do a few other good local dishes, so it's possible to have a substantial meal here as well Nhà hàng Madame Lân ★★★★★ 04 Feb 2026 · ₫200–300k · Lunch 04 Bạch Đằng, Hải Châu, Đà Nẵng 550000, Vietnam Madame Lan is one of Da Nang’s best-known restaurants and popular with both tourists and locals. It’s a large, tastefully designed open-air space and a very pleasant place to eat. The menu offers a good selection of Vietnamese dishes, both regional and from elsewhere in the country. We had a nicely done mì Quảng and a fresh mango salad, but the real standout for me was something I hadn’t had anywhere else: fresh spring rolls filled with turmeric-marinated fish, vermicelli, and coriander, topped with fried dill leaves. That topping is what makes the dish special. The flavours immediately reminded me of chả cá Lã Vọng, but wrapped in rice paper and finished with the fried dill, it works extremely well and feels genuinely distinctive. Easily the highlight of the meal and highly recommended. Prices are very reasonable for such a popular and attractively designed restaurant. Overall, a great choice in Da Nang if you want to try a wide range of Vietnamese dishes in a comfortable setting. DakLac Coffee ★★★★★ 11 Jul 2020 Thắng Lợi, Buon Ma Thuot, Dak Lak, Vietnam It shouldn't come as a surprise that it's easy to get great coffee in Vietnam's coffee capital where it seems almost every other house is a coffee shop. Ngọc Mai Guesthouse ★★☆☆☆ 11 Jul 2020 09 Nguyễn Bính, Thắng Lợi, Buôn Ma Thuột, Đắk Lắk 630000, Vietnam This old school guesthouse would have been perfectly acceptable ten, fifteen years ago when small dark rooms up a long flight of stairs were the norm in cheap traveller joints in Vietnam. However, with the proliferation of modern, comfortable budget hotels all over the country which often offer mid range quality rooms at the same rock bottom prices (the cheapest walk in rate here is 190k) places like this need to either up their game or slash their prices. Hotels in Daklak seem to be slightly pricier than elsewhere in the country, but I'm sure for just 50k more you'll find something much better

PROV: Hà Giang / Đồng Văn
NAME: Pho Co
ADDR: 
TEXT: ★★★★★ 07 Jul 2020 79H7+84R, Nguyễn Trãi, Đồng Văn, Hà Giang, Vietnam There are several sidewalk bbq joints on this street, but Pho Co is by far the most popular. After trying quite a bit of their food, grilled dishes and others I know why. It's not only friendly, but really great quality. It starts with the fact that they serve a really nice buckwheat craft beer (50k) instead of just the usual cheap lagers. The dip that comes with the grilled meat dishes is delicious, a chili sauce with ginger and lime leaf, all home made. There's no industrial meat here either, it's all farmer's meat and hand made sausages, and they're damn tasty, the Hmong sausages (10k a piece) and the charcoal smoked buffalo sausages (50k a piece). They also serve the local specialty Chao Au Tau (35k), a chicken porridge with a special root that is potentially toxic if the cook doesn't know how to prepare it, but apparently it's very healthy when served in the proper way. Mind, you might sit on tiny plastic chairs on the street and get your food served on plastic plates, but this is not cheap food. Even in the Highlands of Northern Vietnam free range meat and craft beers cost money, but the prices here are very reasonable. For 150-200k per person you can have a nice feast here, including drinks. Highly recommended Dong Van Viewpoint - French Fort ★★★★☆ 07 Jul 2020 Đồng Văn, Đồng Văn District, Hà Giang, Vietnam It's a short, but steep hike up to the ruins, which themselves are nothing special, but the views are superb Lam Tung Hotel Đường Phố Cổ kéo dài, Phố Cổ, Đồng Văn, Hà Giang, Vietnam I'm not sure if I'm happy that there's a seven floor hotel right next to the traditional hilltribe market, but to be fair, the location is absolutely perfect and the rooms are good, too. 270k on the weekend for a spacious room with a view, friendly management

Cat Ba Panorama Travel ★★☆☆☆ 22 Jun 2020 53 Núi Ngọc, TT. Cát Bà, Cát Hải, Hải Phòng 180000, Vietnam It's baffling to see all these positive reviews of this operation. I almost wondered if they put me on a bad copycat boat with the same name. But no, it's the same boat as advertised just a lot more shabby. We were promised when booking that things are quiet at the moment and it wouldn't be too busy and that coupled with the fact that this was touted as the luxury option made me book the tour in the first place. What a mistake that was. The boat was packed, they had people sitting on extra plastic chairs for lunch and it wasn't even the weekend. The boat is in deplorable condition, the toilets can't be locked and the upper deck had zero shade because the canopy was broken. This actually turned out to be a saving grace since none of the other guests wanted to sit there, so we got some privacy. But it obviously meant that the lower floors were even more packed. The boat would be comfortable for maybe 20 passengers, fewer than that on a "luxury" tour, but we had at least double that amount. Coffees in the morning and other beverages had to be paid extra and were overpriced (luxury after all). The romantic sunset with complimentary wine started at 2:30 pm and consisted of a small glass of watermelon juice which may or may not have contained a little rice wine. The beach where we stopped for swimming and corals had no corals and it was dirty. 2 stars because lunch was alright (seafood, but the cheap variety) and the guides and staff were nice and professional. But whoever is in charge of this operation should be ashamed to call it a luxury cruise, it would have made just about a barely adequate budget tour. Amendment : Panorama Travel contacted me after reading this review and tried to explain the situation. It seems that due to the Covid19 situation they changed the tour to be more suited to Vietnamese domestic tourism which certainly explains the large number of passengers and less focus on activities such as cycling and swimming. This might change again once the country reopens to Westerners, so take my review as an 'as is' which might improve again in the future Nhat Mai Hotel ★★★★☆ 20 Jun 2020 Nice and friendly family run hotel with spotless and spacious rooms for which are some of the most affordable on the island if you need to stay a night over the weekend. 267k for a room with fridge, setee and a small balcony, ac and WiFi working well. PROV: 41 ngõ 2/238 Đ. Âu Cơ, Quảng An, Tây Hồ, Hà Nội, Vietnam
NAME: Hands down the best beer garden in Hanoi. The location is a bit inconvenient, but it's well worth seeking out. It's the best value craft beer place you'll find in Vietnam. During happy hour from 4-6 pm you get 3 glasses of any Furbrew craft beer for a mere 100k, but even after happy hour prices are reasonable. What makes this place so special though, is the food, which is also excellent value. There's a choice of Central European food prepared by a German chef and Mediterranean food prepared by a Spanish chef. It's a great concept for a beer garden, and I really liked the patatas bravas, the croquetas, the schnitzel and the currywurst. Ironically, you pay less for this kind of food here than you'd pay for local food at some Hanoi local bia hoi joints.
ADDR: Furbrew is not exactly my favourite craft beer in Vietnam, I prefer Turtle Lake and Seven Bridges, but there's a whopping 21 different beers on tap, and some of them are very good.

ADDR: For such a short road, little Đỗ Quang Đẩu in the heart of Saigon's backpacker area, has a good deal of authentic Vietnamese eateries. TEXT: The Vintage Emporium Da Kao ★★★☆☆ 01 Apr 2020 95 Đ. Nguyễn Văn Thủ, Đa Kao, Quận 1, Hồ Chí Minh, Vietnam I'll have to agree with some reviewers here who find this place nice but really overpriced. Now, I'm not one of those silly people who complain that the food here is too expensive for Vietnam, just because they can get some cheap noodles on the street. I know the real estate prices in Saigon, and how much imported ingredients cost, so charging "Western" prices is nothing to complain about. But charging high prices is only justified when you offer high quality, and that's where the Vintage Emporium disappointed a little. The cappuccino for 60k was very good, so no complaints here. However, the Moroccan poached eggs were mediocre. It's fine to charge 160k for 2 eggs, tomato and cheese Moroccan style, if they come in a sumptuous gravy of tomatoes, Harissa and Ras El Hanout, covered with a generous amount of real sheep milk feta, yes that would be a wonderful dish. But what I was served here were two eggs in a relatively bland tomato sauce with just a few tiny cubes of boring cow milk 'feta' on top. It wasn't bad, it's an alright meal, but just not good value and nothing making me crave for more. PROV: Khánh Hòa / Cam Ranh
NAME: Quán Nhậu Thanh Nguyệt
ADDR: 1215 QL1A, khu phố 3, Cam Ranh, Khánh Hòa, Vietnam
TEXT: Accidentally finding a place like this is one of the reasons why travelling around Vietnam is still one of a foodie's life's greatest pleasures. This simple drinking place doesn't even look like a proper eatery from the outside. The location is as bad as it gets, along an industrial, noisy stretch of Highway 1 in the outskirts of non descript Cam Ranh City. We stopped only because they had a bia tuoi sign outside, it was a hot summer day and we were thirsty. Little did we know that we ended up having one of the best meals in a long time here. There's quite an extensive menu of really interesting dishes, not just the usual quan nhau (drinking place) standard fare, and everything is freshly prepared and of very good quality. Their specialties are 'one day sun dried grilled beef with chili ants' and the ridiculously delicious muc/tom mam nhi, essentially raw squid/prawns in a bowl of smooth highest quality fish sauce. Another great and rare dish is their oxtail stew with peanuts. Being close to the sea, it's also no wonder that their grilled fish dishes (ca mu or grouper is always a good choice) are fresh and tasty. All dishes cost less than 100k and a litre of Saigon Bia Hoi is 15k, great value for food of this quality.

PROV: Khánh Hòa / Vạn Ninh
NAME: Giọt đắng coffee
ADDR: 
TEXT: ★★★★☆ 03 Jun 2020 Q8G6+898, Vạn Phước, Vạn Ninh, Khánh Hòa, Vietnam Very pleasant, spacious garden café in an area that's not exactly blessed with them. Good rest stop when you're in the area Kon Tum Gỏi lá Út Cưng 45 Trần Cao Vân, Thống Nhất, Kon Tum, Vietnam Possibly Kontum's most famous restaurant, this large open air place has a very popular version of Goi La, literally leaf salad, which is a specialty in this area. This dish consists of a massive plate of different edible leaves, plus some fillings to wrap around. There's some lard, some prawns, some pork skin, peanuts...and a lovely dipping sauce. Not all the leaves are very tasty, but some have surprisingly distinct and interesting flavours. The whole dish costs less than 100k for 2 and is a must try when you're in the area. For carbs, however, better just order some rice dish, we made the mistake of ordering fries, and they come with sugar instead of salt here. You might think that's a mistake, but the Vietnamese youth actually prefers to eat them that way Quan Cay Sung ĐT672, Xã Đắk Trăm, Đắk Tô, Kon Tum, Vietnam Large simple beer garden and eatery with nice river views. One of the very few places in the area that serves fresh beer. There's some simple dishes, too. PROV: Lào Cai / Bắc Hà
NAME: Phở Bắc Hà Lý Thi
ADDR: 
TEXT: ★★★★☆ 25 Jun 2020 Pạc Kha, TT. Bắc Hà, Bắc Hà, Lào Cai, Vietnam Eating at this place is quite a special experience. With many places in Bac Ha catering mostly to weekend tourist, the old school Ly Thi with its communal wooden tables and shelves stacked with home made rice wine is a very local experience and packed for breakfast even on a regular weekday. Patrons are highlanders of various tribes speaking a wild mix of languages. They do two kinds of pho dishes, using home made purplish pho noodles from red rice. The pho chua (sour Pho) is a very unusual noodle soup which is served cold. A strange choice for a cold place like Bac Ha and while not at all unpleasant I wasn't entirely taken over by its acquired taste. More to my liking was the Pho Tron, a dry noodle dish which comes with hot broth on the side and a choice of pork and chicken which I found very tasty. Price for a bowl is 20 to 30k depending on the meat. Good value. Most patrons drink their home made rice wine, even for breakfast, but we opted to buy some for take away instead. We tried a sampler of four beers—two of which I really liked, while the other two, though not my favorites, were still cheap and refreshing. Even better are their beer cocktails, with big glasses going for under 100k. The biggest surprise, though, is the food. Their Thai-style raw jellyfish and prawn salad (125k) is as good as anything you’d get in Bangkok, and their tapas sampler plate featured some perfectly marinated boiled beef—so this is a bar where you could come just for a good meal as well. I first wrote these lines in May 2019, just a few months before Vietnam was closed off due to the pandemic and Jelly had just opened. It quickly became a meeting spot for stranded backpackers and has since turned into a full-throttle backpacker/expat haven, packed almost every night. Now, in 2025, the beer cocktails are still 90k, and I still enjoy them. The food menu has remained largely the same, too. Louisiane has a very mixed international clientele with a good amount of Vietnamese locals and tourists. There's a pool, and a microbrewery on site which brews some fine beers that are sold at reasonable prices. Happy Hours from 11-13 and 4-6 pm are short but great value. There's a large variety of food which is generally good to excellent, but comes at a price, which is understandable at such a prime location; avoid the pizzas though, they're decidedly mediocre for the price. Update: there's now three happy hours from 11am to 12, 4pm to 5pm and 11pm to midnight. Story and Mangal haven't survived the pandemic, so this is hands down the best beach option in town. 2025 update: no more afternoon happy hour, but longer noon time happy hour from 12-2 with small beers for 45k. They have a new menu with food prices that now rival Sailing Club, but the food quality is really not worth these prices. Fortunately, the beer prices remain reasonable. The dish consists of grilled pork paste, crunchy deep-fried dough, fresh noodles, green mango, pickles, and plenty of herbs and leaves, all wrapped in rice paper. The dipping sauce varies slightly from place to place and is usually a well-kept secret, brewing in a big pot. You mix this lightly sweet sauce with spicy sate, green chili, and garlic for a perfectly balanced, delicious bite. Nha Trang has quite a few nem nướng specialty restaurants, most of them around Dam Market. This little hole-in-the-wall eatery in Backpacker Alley is a convenient option if you want to try nem nướng in the tourist area. It’s obviously not the best in town—the skewers aren’t straight off the grill like in specialty restaurants but are reheated, and the dipping sauce is nothing special. That said, the price is fair (54k for 6), and even average nem nướng is still delicious. Lanterns ★★★★☆ 20 Jun 2019 30A Nguyễn Thiện Thuật, Tân Lập, Nha Trang, Khánh Hòa 650000, Vietnam Lanterns has been Nha Trang's most popular tourist restaurant for many years now but i never really saw why, as i was slightly underwhelmed by my first visit, and especially disappointed by their signature claypot dish, which tasted sweet and boring with medium quality fish. Olivia Restaurant ★★★☆☆ 20 Jun 2019 2 Nguyễn Thiện Thuật, Tân Lập, Nha Trang, Khánh Hòa 650000, Vietnam Olivia has been around and busy for many years which means they must be doing something right. It is indeed a charming, rustic restaurant, certainly one of the more attractive places to eat in Nha Trang's tourist area. However, it's not a place for authentic Italian culinary sensations, i'd be very surprised if they ever had an Italian chef or manager here. The food they serve is tourist Italian for undemanding eaters that fancy pizza and pasta but have never heard of ossobucco or porchetta. Their pizzas are so so, reasonably priced, and definitely not the worst in town. The spinach ravioli 'Boscaiola' were surprisingly nice, they seemed home-made and came with proper cream. The beef carpaccio, however, was a disaster. It was killed by disgusting, cheap olive oil which overpowered all the flavours of the beef and even the parmesan. I would avoid all dishes with olive oil dressing here, they use a really nasty one. Also make sure you avoid their house wine which comes out of a box at Nha Trang room temperature (about 30 degrees). On a positive note, the service here is good and friendly and the menu is still pre-Russian invasion, therefore very reasonably priced (although i'd be willing to pay a little more, so they can afford to use some decent olive oil). Pizza 4P's Sheraton Nha Trang ★★★★★ 06 Apr 2021 Sheraton Hotel, 28 Trần Phú, Lộc Thọ, Nha Trang, Khánh Hòa 57000, Vietnam I'd heard great things about 4P from other people, but it took me a long time to check out what's the hype all about. The main reason was that I'm generally sceptical of restaurants that are located in hotels, especially luxury hotels, since they're often mediocre and overpriced. 4P is different though. It's obviously not a budget eatery, but for the quality they offer here, the prices are surprisingly moderate. You can order most pizzas with their homemade burrata on top, but I would advise against it. Sailing Club Nha Trang ★★★★☆ 20 Jun 2019 72 74 Trần Phú, Lộc Thọ, Nha Trang, Khánh Hòa 570000, Vietnam I first visited the Sailing Club in March 2000, it was a meal I'll never forget. One of the best meals I had in my entire life, and the best meal on a month long foodie trip throughout Vietnam. Back then, it was a much more modest place, but the food was already top notch, and incredible value. On my second visit in 2006, the place had become considerably more posh, but it was still great value for outstanding food and a fantastic atmosphere. But then, in 2006, Nha Trang was paradise on earth, the nightmare it has become still years away. Since I've become more of a local, rather than a tourist in Nha Trang, I haven't really been back often. It's definitely a place for tourists, rather than locals, what with the prices having gone through the roof in recent years. And I don't mean just expensive by Nha Trang standards, it's expensive even by Western standards. The last time I ate there was in 2011, and it was disappointing, nowhere near the quality they had used to offer, and at the price, there's much better food to be had in town. On my last recent visit, I just came for a drink. Admittedly, the atmosphere on a breezy early evening can be magical here, but sorry to say, the prices have become absolutely outrageous. I imagine it's not even their fault, they probably have to pay truckloads of bribes to stay open in this location, but it has really become a one time splurge place for tourists, rather than an everyday place for locals. Sad. Sam Lor Thai Restaurant Nha Trang (Tuktuk) ★★☆☆☆ 14 Apr 2020 76 Đống Đa, Tân Lập, Nha Trang, Khánh Hòa 650000, Vietnam This newly opened Thai restaurant should be so much better. Here it was essentially a salad with plenty of herbs and leaves but only a few crumbs of minced pork on top. Sushi Kiwami Restaurant ★★★★★ 20 Jun 2019 114 Hồng Bàng, Tân Lập, Nha Trang, Khánh Hòa 650000, Vietnam Lucky to have this excellent Japanese run sushi joint in Nha Trang. This competently Japanese-run place is hands down the best sushi place in town. The location is a bit away from the main tourist area, and the place is tiny, but the place has an authentic feel to it, which includes a Japanese chef behind the counter and smoking Japanese patrons in front. This might not be everyone's cup of tea, but in the end it's all about the fresh fish when it comes to sushi and Kiwami delivers the goods. Their nigiri are fresh and succulent with big slices of fish over a small chunk of tasty rice, just the way it should be. The rolls are generous but without sauce or mayo overkill, just the way it should be. Prices are on par with the other sushi bars in town, which makes this one easily the best value, seeing that they offer by far the best quality (Sakura used to be great, but has disappointed me on recent visits). Only drawback is that it has become so popular, it's getting hard to get a table, and opening hours are short. Sushi Samurai ★★☆☆☆ 01 Jul 2019 107 Nguyễn Thiện Thuật, Tân Lập, Nha Trang, Khánh Hòa 650000, Vietnam This Western-owned place has a prime location in the tourist area, is surprisingly inexpensive, and looks good from the outside. Tippy's Mexican Food Nha Trang ★★★☆☆ 11 Mar 2025 65/1 Nguyễn Thiện Thuật, Lộc Thọ, Nha Trang, Khánh Hòa 650000, Vietnam With the sad closure of Los Chilangos, Nha Trang’s only real Mexican restaurant, Tippy’s steps in to fill the gap with decent Tex-Mex—better than many places in Vietnam. Tony Tèo Súp Cua 2 Hoàng Diệu, Vĩnh Hoà, Nha Trang, Khánh Hòa, Vietnam This alley street food place has deservedly become popular for their specialty dish Sup Cua or Crab soup. This kind of soup is very popular with locals all over Vietnam, but it's not very well known among foreigners. This is a pity, and I believe almost anyone trying a bowl here will enjoy it. The basic sup cua (15k) contains shredded chicken, mushrooms and quail eggs in a thick crab meat based broth (hence the name). You can then add other ingredients according to your taste. Fresh prawns, century egg and for the adventurous palate some nice creamy pig brain. An all-in bowl goes for 30k. Add a spoon of their home made chili oil (saté) and you're in heaven. Tony Tèo also serve some other dishes such as Banh Trang Tron (rice paper mango salad, 15-20k) and delicious grilled Bo la lot (20k), plus home made mozzarella sticks and chicken nuggets. If you want to drink some cold beers with your grill and fry platters, they're very accommodating if you bring your own, which makes dining here even less expensive Un In BBQ ★★★★☆ 20 Jun 2019 One of my favourite and best places in NT but for a five star review it lacks consistency. I eat here often and sometimes the food is simply gorgeous. Perfect spicy, fall-off-the-bone ribs, huge portions, fair prices. At other times, however, the ribs are still chewy and the portions are smaller. I'm not sure why this happens because Un In has the potential to be the best value, best loved place to eat in town. I still wholeheartedly recommend the place, it's deservedly popular with locals and foreigners alike, which is rare in Nha Trang. The prices are really fair, even on an off day you still get great value and the fact that it's located by the river, outside of the main tourist area only adds to the appeal. I also recommend ordering some of their Vietnamese dishes as sides, the anchovy salad or bo la lot, they're as good here as in most local places. TEXT: ★★★★☆ 01 Jun 2020 Basic, but very popular Bia Hoi place with a surprisingly varied food menu. The fresh beer is good and cheap, 20k for two litres. Their Bo la lot was great, possibly the best I've ever had. Instead of the usual rolls it came pancake sized on a plate (70k). Lam Sơn, Thanh Hóa, Vietnam Thanh Hoa's most popular Bia hoi joint is worth a visit for the local specialty Nem nuong, which is grilled fermented pork and very fresh beer from the tap. Nhà hàng Đặc Sản Pù Luông ★★★★★ 29 May 2026 Bản Đôn, Pu Luong, Thanh Hoa 40000, Vietnam Pu Luong Auberge is probably the most spectacular restaurant in the province, with absolutely stunning views of the rice terraces and the surrounding mountain range. The setting alone is worth the visit. It’s a large place with a quirky, eclectic interior and even an Italian pizza oven, although I only tried the northern Vietnamese hors d'oeuvre platter and some fried rice, as we were there for brunch and the pizza oven wasn’t operating yet. The food is absolutely fine. It’s nothing particularly outstanding, but that’s not really the point. If you’re in the area, you simply have to stop here, even if it’s only for a drink. The views are amazing, and it’s a place you can’t afford to miss. Best cakes in town, German quality baking Divino italian restaurant pizzeria ★★★★☆ 20 Jun 2019 Fish Island Road, Krong Kampot, Cambodia Now, finding a place like Divino is every travelling foodie's dream. Imagine you find yourself in a sleepy, remote colonial Old Town in the Cambodian province and you stumble over a super casual hole in the wall Italian place and you think, Italian? yeah why not, let's give it a try. Italian is one of the world's cuisines that, due to its popularity, has been messed with the most, and especially in Asia finding the real deal can be a frustrating task. Well, Divino is the real deal. Simple Italian home cooking at its best. They make their own pasta, bake their own delicious bread, every dish is fresh and made from scratch, it's quite wonderful, really. And what's more, they have some excellent Italian wines at bargain prices to complement the dishes. Prices for food and drinks are a steal, with most mains and pasta dishes under 5$. We had carpaccio, ravioli and gnocchi, and they were all delicious. It should be 5 stars, really. However, i was a little disappointed with the pizza i ordered, which is strange and unnecessary since they got the hard part right. The dough was perfectly baked, thin, crispy and flavoursome, just the way it should be, it was the topping the fell flat. I know imported ingredients are very expensive in Cambodia and the large Pizza Napoli goes for only 5$ but maybe it would be better to charge 7$ and put some more cheese and anchovies because, while i dislike overloaded pizzas, a little more toppings would have made it much nicer. Enough said. When you're in Kampot and you like food, don't give Divino a miss. We ordered some Khmer standard dishes such as raw beef salad, banana blossom and raw fish salad, as well as chicken curry. They all came across as authentic and flavourful, the way these dishes would be served in a local Khmer beer garden without English menu. And i mean that as a compliment. The beef salad in particular stood out for the excellent quality of the meat. Another dish we ordered is less common in Cambodia, but living in Vietnam i was pleased to see the beef wrapped in betel leaves on the menu, one of my favourite dishes in Vietnam, and the taste was just perfect, juicy and delicious. With most dishes between 5-10 $ Mok Mony is not cheap but reasonably priced and good value, and definitely a great place for newcomers to sample Khmer cuisine, but even jaded expats will be able to appreciate the quality of the food. Chanrey Tree ★★★☆☆ 20 Jun 2019 Mondul 1 Village, Svay Dangkum Commune, Pokambor Ave, Krong Siem Reap 17252, Cambodia Chanrey Tree is a remarkably beautiful restaurant, from the lotus pond entrance to the minimalist lemongrass scented ac dining room. It must be an amazing experience for first time travellers of the region to eat in a restaurant which fulfills all the romantic clichés of a trip to Indochina, all in swanky clean surroundings. They might even think the wine list is reasonably priced, when in fact it is terribly overpriced for Siem Reap with the cheapest house wine starting at almost 30$. The food at Chanrey Tree is beautifully presented, but taste wise it's pretty ordinary. Most dishes are around 10$ and portions are quite generous, so the price would be alright if the quality matched the exquisite surroundings. However, out of three dishes we ordered, only one was really good. The seafood with Kampot pepper was fresh and the sauce delicious. Verdict: A very beautiful place to eat, and most likely a great experience for people unfamiliar with the finer details of Khmer cooking. For foodies with knowledge of Khmer cuisine, however, this place is definitely style over substance. There are better fine dining options in town. Be aware that they're one of the very few restaurants outside the big hotels in Siem Reap that add 10% service charge to your bill. The Crocodile River “schnitzel vanna” ★★★★☆ 03 Jul 2019 Concrete Drain Rd, Krong Siem Reap, Cambodia If you're seriously hungry, give this one a try This is a simple outdoor place by the river a bit south of town. Curry Walla ★☆☆☆☆ 20 Jun 2019 Sivatha Rd, Krong Siem Reap, Cambodia It needs to be said that Curry Walla used to be my favourite Indian restaurant in Siem Reap, and I've had countless takeaways and was never disappointed. Until one day when they plain and simple cheated me when I ordered Chicken Tikka Masala and Lamb Korma for take away. The chicken was chewy and dry, tikka cannot possibly be chewy and dry, the definition of tikka and the reason it's generally more expensive than regular chicken, is that it's marinated, boneless and tender. So basically the Chicken Tikka Masala was just a regular cheap chicken curry, Worse though was the 'lamb' korma. It's an expensive dish at around 9$, which is fair enough because lamb is rare and expensive in Cambodia. What's not okay is to replace expensive lamb with cheap beef and sell it as lamb. That's just disrespecting your customers and also plain and simple cheating. I'm not a fool, i can taste the difference between lamb and beef. Luckily, i'm not a Hindu hehe Anyway, i've since found a new Indian place to frequent in Siem Reap, I will never go back to Curry Walla. Da. Roberto L'Oasi Italiana ★★★★☆ 02 Jul 2019 ផ្លូRiver Side ភូមិទ្រាំង សង្កាត់ស្ល ក្រាម ក្រុងសៀមរាប ខេត្តសៀមរាប ក្រុងសៀមរាប, 17251, Cambodia Da Roberto is located in a lovely little grove just outside Siem Reap and definitely worth the short trip out of town. Footprint Cafes ★★★★☆ 26 Jun 2019 Postal Code 17254, Street 26, Wat Bo, Village, Krong Siem Reap, Cambodia Footprint is a friendly little book café with excellent coffee and very decent Khmer bistro food. Mamma Shop Italian Restaurant 678 Hap Guan St, Krong Siem Reap 17252, Cambodia The aptly named Mamma Shop is a small, cute Italian place with some of the best Italian food you will find in this country. It's a bit off the main tourist area, but it's deservedly popular for the quality of the food and the moderate prices. Every dish i ordered on two visits was excellent. Deceptively easy dishes such as carpaccio or pasta dishes are often the hardest to get just right, and Mamma Shop delivers on both occasions. The beef carpaccio (6$) was perfect, paper thin slices of meat on a subtle dressing topped with crunchy rucola and parmesan. Delicious. The ravioli pomodoro (7$) were totally convincing as well, al dente, homemade with a fresh, tasty sauce. The pizzas (5-7$) are excellent, you won't get any better in a good pizzeria in Italy. Proper Southern style with generous toppings without being overloaded. Perfect. Now, the only reason i can't give five stars is that they messed up my take away pizza. I ordered a Pizza Prosciutto Parma e Rucola which, as the name implies, should contain parma ham and rocket. The pizza was very good, no doubt, with plenty of Parma ham, but i discovered at home that the Rucola was missing. However, when i ordered, nobody told me they had run out. So maybe somebody just forgot to put it. Anyway, rocket gives the pizza the necessary zest and is almost indispensable for this type of pizza, so there was quite a bit of a loss of quality without it. Which is a shame because Mamma Shop is a wonderful little restaurant with great food and fair prices. But i only give 5 stars to perfect meals, hence the deduction. Olive Cuisine de Saison ★★★★★ 30 May 2021 Olive St, Krong Siem Reap 17252, Cambodia Olive - Cuisine de Saison is a very attractive fine dining restaurant in Siem Reap's Old Town. Its dining room is nicely designed and comfortable, fancy yet casual. The menu is Mediterranean with emphasis on French and some Asian influences. I was extremely happy to see ris de veau (calf sweetbreads) on the menu, a delicacy which is very rare in South East Asia (unfortunately on my last visit no more here either). We ordered four dishes. A fantastic beef carpaccio with rucola and parmesan, a very generous portion. Tuna Avocado tartare, a classic dish, which tasted very fresh with crunchy fresh Kampot pepper Pasta with sweetbreads and morilles, which is of course not a cheap dish (17.50$) but you get a lot of delicious meat and the cream sauce was not overpowering. And last a salad with oven baked prawns and avocados. The prawns were just perfect and the dressing very nice. I simply couldn't find any fault in the food, everything was impeccable, generous and well priced. The wine list is still improvable, it's quite short, especially for whites, and pricier than in similar restaurants in Siem Reap with the cheapest bottle of house wine over 20$. You did, however, get a small bowl of olives complimentary with the wine which is a nice touch. Palate Angkor Restaurant & Bar ★★★★☆ 03 Jul 2019 Along Siem Reap River, Acha Sva Road, Corner Street 20, Krong Siem Reap, Cambodia Attractive, upmarket Khmer fusion restaurant by the river. Food comes tapas size as well and is reasonably priced. Decent wine list, good service, and 3 out of 4 dishes were very good. Recommended Red Piano Sok San ★★★★☆ 26 Jun 2019 Sok San Rd, Krong Siem Reap, Cambodia The cappuccino at Red Piano is a little underwhelming considering the 2–2.50$ price tag, especially since there are much better cafés in Siem Reap. Their Khmer lunch specials, however, usually come with a free beer and are very good value, with generous portions and surprisingly decent quality. Slatoum Restaurant by Rohatt Cafe ★★★★☆ 03 Jul 2019 Road # 27, Wat Bo Village, Sangkat Salaubrouk, 17253, Cambodia The coffee and cocktails at Slatoum were fairly average and didn't leave much of an impression, but the beef lok lak was genuinely outstanding. Perfectly peppery, with tender cubes of beef and exactly the kind of flavour the dish should have. The restaurant itself is pleasant enough overall, so four stars still feels fair. Taj Mahal ★★★☆☆ 26 Jun 2019 Street No.2, 17252, Cambodia Despite the Indian owners, the North Indian dishes here taste rather different from the real thing, possibly because the kitchen seems more South Indian influenced. The food is still perfectly tasty, just not especially authentic. On the plus side, the draft beer used to be absurdly cheap at around 25 cents. Temple Coffee n Bakery 9V45+269, Street 25 Archbishop Mondulkov, Krong Siem Reap 17253, Cambodia Temple Coffee has fantastic décor and is one of the most comfortable café-lounge spaces in Siem Reap. The coffee is good, and they also serve a surprisingly nice range of inexpensive international finger food such as sliders, salmon rolls, and beef tartare. The local dishes are less memorable, but still decent enough. Temple Food n Beverage ★★★☆☆ 26 Jun 2019 Mondul 1 Village Street 08 Siem Reap, 17252, Cambodia Part of the Temple café group, this branch does at least serve beer at extremely low prices. The menu, however, is fairly limited and not especially cheap. The fish amok was decent enough but not convincing enough to make me want to return specifically for the food. Touich Restaurant wat Enkosei- Trang village- Slorkram commune 60 Angkor Tree Street ក្រុងសៀមរាប, 17251, Cambodia Touich absolutely deserves its reputation and is well worth leaving the centre of town for. This is Khmer cuisine done properly, with beautifully presented versions of all the classics, excellent service, and prices that remain surprisingly affordable for the quality. V Design Restaurant ★★★★☆ 26 Jun 2019 Mondulkiri Village ផ្លូវលេខ ០៨ siem reap, Siem, Reap 17252, Cambodia V Design is probably the most comfortable place around Pub Street to sit down for a while. Cheap ice-cold beers are a given, but the food is genuinely good too. The seafood amok in particular is excellent value, with portions large enough for two people to share comfortably. Vanakkam India ★★★☆☆ 02 Jul 2019 Opposite provincial hospital, near by, 2 Thnou St, Krong Siem Reap, Cambodia Vanakkam is a friendly and slightly more polished-looking Indian restaurant than many others in Siem Reap. The food is perfectly tasty, but not especially memorable considering the above-average prices. With so many Indian restaurants in town, I never really felt the urge to return. Viva Mexico and Khmer Restaurant #139+141, Street Sisowath (#1, Cambodia Viva is an institution! They've been serving their 5$ mango margarita pitchers in Siem Reap and Phnom Penh for well over a decade without raising their prices. Their Khmer food is tasty and reliable, i like their version of fish amok a lot. The "Mexican" is basic Tex-Mex, but it's alright, filling, and goes well with cold beers or margaritas. I never miss an opportunity to visit Viva when I'm in town Sihanoukville · 16 reviews The Big Easy ★★★★☆ 20 Jun 2019 800 Mittapheap Street, Preah Sihanouk, Cambodia The Big Easy follows more or less the same formula as Monkey Republic next door, but somehow seems considerably more popular these days. Cheap drinks, long happy hours, and good music still work perfectly well in Sihanoukville. BoBi Coffee & Green Tea ★★★☆☆ 20 Jun 2019 ផ្លូវ ៧ មករា, Preah Sihanouk, Cambodia BoBi is a spacious and comfortable café with modern Asian-style décor and plenty of colourful seating. Del Mar Pastry & Coffee ★★★★☆ 20 Jun 2019 198, Ekareach str Sihanoukville, 18000, Cambodia Out of the many modern air-conditioned cafés that have opened in Sihanoukville in recent years, Del Mar is probably my favourite overall. It is slightly more polished and expensive than most competitors, but the cappuccino is also one of the best in town, even at around 2.50$. Enocafe Coffee & Italian Restaurant ★★★★☆ 20 Jun 2019 Koh toch village Koh toch village, Koh Rong commune, Koh Rong Island, Preah Sihanouk, Cambodia Their Italian cappuccino is actually not better than at some of the other coffee shops in town, but it's OK for 2$. Greenhouse Effect ★★★★☆ 20 Jun 2019 HGGX+JCQ, Preah Sihanouk, Cambodia Greenhouse Effect feels a little worn around the edges these days, but the atmosphere is still very good. Drinks are reasonably priced, although charging 2$ for a coconut feels slightly optimistic even by beach standards. The views are excellent, though. Khin's Shack ★★★★★ 20 Jun 2019 Preah Sihanouk, Cambodia Khin's Shack feels like one of the last survivors of the old Otres Beach atmosphere before Sihanoukville changed beyond recognition. Cheap drinks, wicker chairs in the sand, fresh seafood barbecue, and genuinely relaxed old-school beach vibes. The large seafood BBQ platter at around 12$ is excellent value. Hopefully the place survives. LOTUS Restaurant ★★★★☆ 04 Jul 2019 Holiday Palace Hotel 2 Thnou Street, Independence beach Sihanoukville, 18000, Cambodia LOTUS claims to serve the best dim sum in Sihanoukville and, surprisingly enough, that claim is probably justified. The baskets are inexpensive at around 1.25–1.75$ and the quality is genuinely good. Slightly ironic perhaps that, with Sihanoukville increasingly dominated by Chinese development, one of the better meals in town is still at a Chinese restaurant. Moorea Beach ★★★★☆ 04 Jul 2019 HGJW+2CP, Preah Sihanouk, Cambodia Moorea is probably my favourite place around Otres Beach. Very comfortable cushions, tasteful design, decent chilled wine, and food that remains reasonably priced despite the setting. The swordfish sashimi goes particularly well with a glass of white Minervois. Otres Boat Club ★★★★☆ 20 Jun 2019 Marina Rd, Preah Sihanouk 18000, Cambodia Otres Boat Club has an excellent beachfront location with comfortable cushions right by the water. The setup is more relaxed and less pretentious than some nearby beach clubs, and prices are correspondingly more reasonable. Happy hour runs from 4 to 7 pm. PALAIS COFFEE ★★★☆☆ 04 Jul 2019 2 THNOU STREET, INDEPENDENCE BEACH SIHANOUKVILLE, 18000, Cambodia Coffee quality here is somewhat inconsistent compared with the better café chains, but finding a genuinely decent cappuccino in Sihanoukville has never been easy. At around 2$, the cappuccino here is still one of the more acceptable options in town. Sandan ★★★★☆ 02 Jul 2019 lit mango tree, Street 10311 one block south of 7 Makara Street (look for our brightly, Preah Sihanouk, Cambodia Just like all 'good cause' restaurants Sandan is of course overrated (people always seem to give extra points for good causes instead of focusing on what counts, food, service, atmosphere...). However, the food at Sandan is indeed very good, not outstanding, but good quality Khmer fare. Some dishes can be ordered as half portions which is a nice touch and makes it easier to sample more different things. The beef salad, seafood amok, squid with Kampot pepper were all flawless, the beef curry had fatty meat pieces which shouldn't be found in a 6$ curry. And that brings us to the few negative things that can be said about Sandan. It's not exactly good value, 9$ for a seafood amok is downright expensive despite the good quality. And the service is not very good either, the students were sluggish and inattentive, without the excellent supervisor it would have been a disaster. Happy hour for drinks by the glass from 5-7pm, daiquiris are a bit on the sweet side but quite delicious. All in all, Sandan is a very nice restaurant that is worth a visit, but you should know that you'll find Khmer food of the same quality for less money elsewhere in town. Sihanoukville's fanciest seafood restaurant ★★★★★ 21 Jun 2019 his is probably Sihanoukville's fanciest and best restaurant but given the amazing location and the quality of the food, the prices are reasonable. I've eaten here three times in the past 18 months and never had a single disappointing dish. The 'Deck Bites' are a great way of sampling what's on offer, other outstanding dishes are the wonton duck consomée and (when available) the lamb. The best place for a splurge and a must for every foodie visiting S'ville. Sofinny Restaurant ★★★★☆ 20 Jun 2019 HHC4+8X5, Preah Sihanouk, Cambodia Sofinny is a very good choice in Otres Village for inexpensive, home-style Khmer cooking with genuinely nice flavours throughout. The crab dishes are especially worth ordering. Stray Cats Guesthouse ★★★★☆ 20 Jun 2019 HH95+XHJ, Otres Village, Preah Sihanouk, Cambodia Stray Cats has a relaxed little lounge atmosphere, cheap drinks, and a surprisingly good local restaurant attached to it. The Khmer dishes, especially things like Kampot pepper crab fresh from the wok, are excellent value. Best stick with the local food, though, since the Mexican dishes are much less convincing. Twin Lotus Restaurant ★★☆☆☆ 20 Jun 2019 JG9H+F7G, វិថី ឯករាជ្យ ១០០, Preah Sihanouk, Cambodia Twin Lotus looks polished and rather upscale by Sihanoukville standards, but the experience didn't really justify the prices. A fairly average cappuccino costs 2.70$, and the dish we actually wanted to order was unavailable. Overall not particularly impressive. ផ្ទះខ្មែរ Otres's Steak House ★★★★☆ 20 Jun 2019 Preah Sihanouk, Cambodia This place feels slightly more refined than most restaurants around Otres Village, with proper napkins, a wine fridge, and a generally more polished atmosphere. The Khmer food is genuinely good, seafood especially, and mains remain reasonably priced at around 5$. Charging 2$ for canned juice is pushing it a bit, though.

But what happened next is unforgivable. I ordered a cappuccino for dine in, and it came in a plastic cup with cinnamon on top. With a name like La Bella, you would expect at least a small amount of Italian café culture, and that certainly doesn't involve plastic cups and cinnamon. Also, in both Italy and the Philippines it is customary to offer a glass of complimentary drinking water with your coffee, but here they flatly refused and said we could buy their bottled water. PROV: Davao / Davao City · 9 reviews
NAME: Belito's
ADDR: 
TEXT: ★★★★☆ 25 Apr 2021 Palm Dr, Bajada, Davao City, Davao del Sur, Philippines I had read about Belito's in a food blog, but only decided to visit after the personal recommendation of Samal Island's best chef. Belito's Vineyard is actually located just off busy Laurel St, but its rustic garden setting makes you feel a thousand miles removed from hectic city life. The restaurant itself is a simple affair with plastic chairs and wooden tables, not everything on the menu was available and not even their white wines were pre-chilled but the fact that they had some real quality wines at rock bottom prices, and that all the dishes that eventually came out were excellent, made you easily forgive these small inadequacies. We started with a nice chicken paté, followed by the delicious shrimp Kinilaw. For mains we had the squid in its ink and one of the best lenguas i've ever tried. The only dish that wasn't fully satisfying was the lamb stew. The lamb was nicely cooked but putting synthetic cheese on top wasn't the best idea (very Pinoy style though). The homemade durian ice cream for dessert was quite sublime. Prices for both food and wine are very reasonable and you'd be hard pressed to find better Spanish-Filipino food in Davao, well, Tiny Kitchen is just as good but Belito's has a better atmosphere by far, and they serve wine. Blugre Coffee ★★★☆☆ 04 Jul 2019 Abreeza Mall, J.P. Laurel Ave, Bajada, Davao City, 8000 Davao del Sur, Philippines Blugre is a pleasant enough café, but putting cinnamon on a cappuccino remains an unforgivable offence in my book. The more interesting reason to come here is probably the novelty durian coffee, which is at least something a bit different. Bulgogi Brothers Korean Bbq Restaurant ★★★★☆ 04 Jul 2019 Fountain Court, SM Lanang Premier, J.P. Laurel Ave, Lanang, Davao City, 8000 Davao del Sur, Philippines Bulgogi Brothers is one of those reliable Korean franchises where you more or less know what you're going to get. The food is good, portions are generous, prices are reasonable, and in a city like Davao it's a very welcome option to have. Claude's Le Cafe de Ville ★★★★★ 28 May 2021 The Oboza Heritage House, 143 Rizal St, Poblacion, Lungsod ng Dabaw, 8000 Lalawigan ng Davao del Sur, Philippines Claude's Café de Ville is a magnificent restaurant housed in an old mansion right in the busy city centre. It's a beautiful and tasteful oasis in a dusty, chaotic area of town. And the beauty of it all, the quality of the food actually matches the surroundings. It's such a pleasant surprise to find authentic, classy French food in this little corner of the world. During the holiday season Claude offers some really rare treats such as calf's head or couscous royale (with delicious merguez) on top of his standard menu. The foie gras at Claude's is small and pricy but truly sublime, certainly one of the best i've had in the Philippines. And i found the other items on his menu reasonably priced for the quality offered. The only negative thing i could say about Claude's is that the wine list is exclusively French and therefore bad value. The house wine is good but at a hefty 1150 Php it better be and there are no better value new world wines on the menu. Nevertheless, the existence of a gem like Claude's in this remote, underappreciated city is very appreciated. Nonki Japanese Restaurant (Davao) ★★★☆☆ 04 Jul 2019 AutoVille Building, F. Torres St, Poblacion District, Davao City, 8000 Davao del Sur, Philippines Nonki is probably the most popular Japanese restaurant in Davao, but I found the quality rather average considering the prices. The sashimi and rolls were perfectly acceptable, just not nearly good enough to justify what they charge. Roadhouse Café - SM City, Ecoland Davao City ★★★★☆ 28 May 2021 SM CITY DAVAO Building, Corner Tulip Drive, Quimpo Boulevard, Ecoland, Davao City, 8000 Davao del Sur, Philippines This restaurant at SM City is the Filipino version of an American diner. That means they serve honest local food in big portions at decent prices. I was actually surprised that the quality of the food here was so good, it even made me return to try a couple of more dishes. All the dishes we ordered, the tangigue kinilaw, the stuffed calmar, the kare-kare and the seafood basket were all impeccable. If Filipino food was promoted worldwide by quality mall franchises such as Roadhouse, it would certainly have a much better reputation, because there are enough excellent local dishes in this country, it's just not so easy to find them prepared well. Prices are on the high side for Davao city but for the size and quality still very reasonable, so if you're in the Ecoland area, give this one a try, you might be positively surprised. The Swiss Deli & Restaurant - Matina ★★★★☆ 30 May 2021 La Cima, 1 Gen. Douglas MacArthur Hwy, Talomo, Davao City, 8000 Davao del Sur, Philippines First of all, I want to say that Swiss Deli is an absolute godsent in Davao, their deli shop being the only place where you can find quality European (and local) delicacies in this part of the world, some of it at a fraction of the price you'd pay for the same quality in Europe. Now for the food in the restaurant (i went to the Matina branch). It's simple, unpretentious Pan-European food, nothing outstanding but inexpensive, tasty and good value. We tried the Ravioli which were okay, a nice seafood risotto, fish terrine and very tasty French onion soup. All of this with a bottle of nice Chilean white came to less than 1500 Php, a real steal, especially for wines, which you can buy at the deli shop and consume for a small corkage fee. Good service by Filipino standards, but the ambiance is more canteen than cozy restaurant. Tiny Kitchen & Dulce Vida ★★★★☆ 28 May 2021 F. Torres St, Poblacion District, Davao City, Davao del Sur, Philippines Frankly, this is a terrible restaurant, it's cramped and designed like a cafeteria and the patrons seem to consist exclusively of rude, arrogant old family types who have been running and ruining this country for centuries. However, there is a very good reason to come here, the Spanish-Filipino food they serve here is quite delicious and the waitresses, while not very competent, try their best to make you feel comfortable. Out of their extensive menu featuring most classics and some innovations, we chose the delicious calamares rellenos en su tinta, the callos tripe stew and the braised tongue lengua estofado. Most dishes are under 300 Php, portions are big and the food is really tasty. They don't seem to serve wine there, but i didn't ask for corkage fees, so if you come here for dinner maybe it's a good idea to call ahead and bring your own. The White House ★★★☆☆ 28 May 2021 3JW7+8WC, Camella Northpoint, J.P. Laurel Ave, Buhangin, Lungsod ng Dabaw, Lalawigan ng Davao del Sur, Philippines Fine dining pretend The White House is a beautiful restaurant in a heritage building with a show kitchen and all the trappings of a fine dining establishment. The atmosphere is excellent, but for everything else, from service to food, there's still room for improvement. It started pretty badly when my choice of wine (one of the house wines) was not available. This should not happen in a restaurant with high ambitions. But in a real fine dining restaurant with a good management, had such a faux pas occurred, it would have been fixed by a complimentary upgrade to the next bottle of the same grape and country of origin. Problem solved, customer happy. But here the clueless waitress suggested me a bottle with completely different characteristics than the one i asked for. Again, this should not happen, if you don't have a clue, don't make recommendations. Anyway, we finally ordered our food, one menu 'Alsace', salmon sashimi and the trio of foie gras (let me check if this is available first, sir...hum). The food at the White House is interesting and creative, Japanese-Mediterranean fusion, and it's obvious that the young chef is talented and bold, even if not all dishes worked well (foie gras and blue cheese don't go together well). I really enjoyed the salmon sashimi, the glazed pork belly and the japanese cheesecake. The biggest disappointment was the aforementioned foie gras which i'd really been looking forward to, but which simply didn't work for me. Prices for food and wine are reasonable for such a fancy restaurant and the quality of the ingredients, however, service and consistency of the food could and should be improved

PROV: Davao / Samal Island · 1 review
NAME: Bahay Cubo Restaurant and Bar
ADDR: 
TEXT: ★★★★★ 28 May 2021 3PG3+X4V, Samal, Davao del Norte, Philippines Okay, let's face it, Samal island is a beautiful place but it's not a place for foodies. For nice wine and good food it's usually necessary to take the ferry over to Davao. Fortunately, there is Alphonse and Jaqueline's Bahay Kubo, a hidden gem, that is a must for everyone visiting Samal island. This is not your average restaurant, though. It's only open Fri Sat Sun, and it's a labour of love rather than a business. There's no menu, Alphonse will offer you whatever is available, usually some nice choices of different meat and fish dishes, soup and dessert. Whatever will be served to you is not fancy food, this is a simple place on a simple island, but the quality, the preparation and the freshness is simply outstanding. The tuna steak was perfectly cooked and truly divine, the roast beef melted in your mouth and the beef meatballs with fried potatoes were some of the best i had in Asia, They also boast a nice variety of good value quality wines, mainly from Chile, perfectly chilled, a true godsent in this part of the world. The only downside to Bahay Kubo is the fact that they're only open on the weekends, so we only managed to eat there twice. If you're in Samal on a weekend, no matter where you stay, get yourself to Fernandez Beach (Google maps) and follow the signs, you will not regret it.

PROV: Metro Manila / BGC (Taguig) · 19 reviews
NAME: Brothers Burger - Bonifacio High Street
ADDR: 
TEXT: ★★★★☆ 16 Jun 2019 B5, Bonifacio High Street High Street, Taguig, 1634 Metro Manila, Philippines Brothers Burger is still probably the best burger franchise in the Philippines. Unlike many local chains, they thankfully avoid putting sweetness into the buns or mayo, and the burgers have proper texture and flavour. The lamb burger is especially good and worth the roughly 250 Php price tag. Always a reliable favourite. Crystal Jade Dining IN ★★★★☆ 21 Jun 2019 H22X+7P3, Bonifacio High Street, 7th Ave, Taguig, Metro Manila, Philippines The main reason to visit any Crystal Jade branch is usually the dim sum, and this one is no exception. The BGC branch is more polished and upscale than most, with prices to match. The dim sum selection is not huge, but the quality is consistently very good. At around 200 Php a basket it feels expensive, but proper dim sum options in Manila are surprisingly limited, and Crystal Jade is probably still among the best. Din Tai Fung ★★★★★ 20 Jun 2019 L/G C1, Bonifacio High Street Central, Taguig, Metro Manila, Philippines This branch delivers the usual Din Tai Fung standard, with excellent dumplings and surprisingly reasonable prices for BGC. It gets extremely busy during meal times though, so waiting for a table is almost inevitable. Kuppa Roastery & Cafe ★★★☆☆ 03 Jul 2019 H23W+FXQ, 4th Ave, Taguig, Metro Manila, Philippines Kuppa uses good espresso beans and the coffee preparation itself is perfectly competent, but the milk tasted unpleasantly stale and ruined the overall cup. Which is a shame, because the lamb caldereta was excellent and very good value by BGC standards. Unfortunately I came for the coffee, and that part disappointed. L'entrecôte ★★★☆☆ 03 Jul 2019 Forbestown Rd, Taguig, Metro Manila, Philippines The food at L'entrecôte is good and the wine list is thoughtfully put together, but for this price level the restaurant lacks both polish and a real wow factor. Service feels less professional than it should, and serving oysters with Tabasco because there is no mignonette available is a fairly baffling move for a French restaurant. Lorenzo's Way ★★★★☆ 02 Jul 2019 2nd Level, C2, 7th Ave, Taguig, Metro Manila, Philippines Lorenzo's Way has been serving very solid upscale Filipino food for years and remains deservedly popular. Prices are high, but the quality is there. The lengua was excellent, although the callos leaned a little too salty for my taste. Best visited outside peak hours when the atmosphere is more relaxed. Lugang Cafe SM Aura ★★★☆☆ 21 Jun 2019 Sm Aura Premier, 5/L McKinley Pkwy, Taguig, 1634 Metro Manila, Philippines This outlet in SM Aura' Skypark looks very inviting with its chandeliers and show kitchen. The menu is very extensive but we limited ourselves to a variety of their Shanghai style dumplings. The problem with Lugang is that they don't have any samplers or small orders available, and every serving consists of 8 big dumplings. So this is not a place for solo diners or couples unless you're absolutely starved. That is a real shame because the dumplings are nice and would have loved to try all the different varieties. Prices seem steep but considering the size of the portions it's reasonable. The service, however, is very poor and quite unable to cope during busy times. Max's Restaurant ★★★★☆ 02 Jul 2019 Center, 26th Street Forbestown Rd, Taguig, 1634 Metro Manila, Philippines Whenever I end up at Max's, it's usually for two things: the chicken sisig and the mango shakes. Both are genuinely excellent and among my favourite versions anywhere in the Philippines. The rest of the menu doesn't really interest me nearly as much. Murray D'Vine Ph ★★★★☆ 03 Jul 2019 space c114, ground floor Retail area, Taguig, 1634 Metro Manila, Philippines Probably the best bar around High Street for happy hour. Drinks specials are good, beers come properly ice cold, and the atmosphere is lively without trying too hard. PAUL Boulangerie et Patisserie ★★★★☆ 03 Jul 2019 G/F Bench Tower, Rizal Drive Cor 30th Street, Bonifacio Global City, Rizal Drive, Taguig, 1634 Kalakhang Maynila, Philippines The bread at PAUL is extremely expensive by Manila standards, but the quality is genuinely on par with what you would get in France. The Flûte Charlemagne in particular is excellent. One of the few places in the city where the bakery actually lives up to the French branding. Lartizan ★★★★☆ 04 Jul 2019 Serendra 2 Loading Bay, Ground, 26th corner McKinley Pkwy, Metro Manila, Philippines Lartizan goes heavily for the rococo aesthetic, all ornate crockery, silver cutlery, and slightly theatrical presentation. The chicken foie gras pâté makes an excellent breakfast and is easily large enough for two people. Coffee is good, bread quality is high, and despite appearances the place is not quite as expensive as it first seems. The pretzels, however, are best avoided. Service is friendly, if somewhat clueless. RUE Forbes town, BGC ★★★★☆ 01 Apr 2020 Unit 153, Forbes Town Center, 29th St, Taguig, 1634, Philippines I somehow keep ending up at RUE whenever I go out in BGC. The atmosphere is loud and chaotic, but generally good natured and fun. Drinks are expensive, as expected in this area, but the place itself doesn't feel overly pretentious. The nachos supreme are particularly good. Las Flores ★★★★☆ 20 Jun 2019 One McKinley Place, 25th St, Taguig, 1634 Metro Manila, Philippines Las Flores is a good looking, modern restaurant with good service and a classic (one might say unadventurous) menu which includes most of our favourite small plates. Among the five dishes that we ordered, none stood out and none fell flat, it was all tasty, well prepared and nice to look at. Scallop ceviche with jamón, tuna escabeche (big portion!), pulpo gallega (tender)...all very nice. The beef with porcini and pine nuts could have done with more mushrooms, but it was good nevertheless. Their mango tatin is recommended for dessert, an easy winner in the country with the best mangoes in the world. With tapas prices around 400 Php, Las Flores is pricey even by BGC standards but they have some good lunch deals, as well as a very reasonably priced and extensive wine list which almost makes up for it. Single Origin - Bonifacio High Street ★★★★☆ 20 Jun 2019 C3, Bonifacio Highstreet, 7th Ave, Taguig, 1634 Metro Manila, Philippines The first time I visited here, they had just newly opened. It had a lot of potential, as well as some teething problems. Good service, quality products, but the cappuccino was served too hot and the flat bread dough should have been crispier. They seem to have better baristas these days. Coffee drinks are very good now, but it's expensive. Flat white is 160 Php Toby's Estate Coffee Roasters ★★★★☆ 20 Jun 2019 G/F, Shangri-la at the Fort, Bonifacio High Street, Taguig, Metro Manila, Philippines Excellent coffees (147 Php for cappuccino), some comfy seats with plugs, but oddly no wifi. Usually busy UCC Mentore Coffee + Bar ★★★☆☆ 03 Jul 2019 Second Floor, Sm Aura Premier, Taguig, Metro Manila, Philippines UCC Mentore is definitely expensive, but at least the coffee is noticeably better than the Starbucks downstairs. They also have wifi, which already gives them an advantage over quite a few cafés in BGC. Village Tavern ★★★★☆ 21 Jun 2019 2/F Bonifacio High Street Central, 7th Ave, Taguig, Kalakhang Maynila, Philippines Village Tavern is a surprisingly good option on Bonifacio High. It's a classic American diner with a slightly upmarket menu full of comfort food with options ranging from Pacific-rim to Tex-Mex to Continental. It's worth visiting for their goat cheese - chorizo spring rolls alone, but i also thoroughly enjoyed the shrimp balls and the ox cheeks, everything we tried, in fact. High street prices, yes, but portions are generous, and their house wine is an affordable, but nice Italian Trebbiano, so it's not bad value at all. You should come hungry, though. I was also quite impressed by the service, which was very attentive by Filipino standards. Wildflour Restaurant - BGC ★★★★★ 04 Jul 2019 Ground Floor Six/NEO 4th Avenue, Corner 26th St, Taguig, Metro Manila, Philippines Knowing the average Filipino palate, i'm seriously surprised by the ridiculous popularity of this place, which makes it next to impossible to get a place here most of the time. The bread is absolutely delicious, crispy without a hint of doughy sweetness. The cappuccino is perfectly prepared and super strong, no cinammon or other atrocities done to it. This is so fundamentally different from what you usually get in this country, but it's good to see that it is accepted and received well. Hopefully this will show other restaurateurs that you can offer quality without watering it down to average people's standard tastes and still be wildly popular. I haven't tried enough of their food menu to comment much on it, but it seems to be interesting, if expensive bistro fare and I very much enjoyed the chorizo-figs-bacon wraps, served with plenty of that to-die-for baguette. Their croissant sandwiches are very nice, too. Yoree Korean Dining ★★★☆☆ 15 Jul 2019 1-5 Forum 7th Avenue cor, 25th St, Taguig, Metro Manila, Philippines The food and service at Yoree are both perfectly good, but I'm not entirely convinced by the value for money. The BBQ meat portions were surprisingly small, and the octopus stew contained very little octopus considering the prices they charge.

Wooden Spoon ★★★★☆ 26 Jun 2019 P1 Power Plant Mall Cor Estrella St, 1210 Rockwell Dr, Makati, Metro Manila, Philippines Good modern takes on Filipino classics in a pleasant setting. Oarhouse Pub of Manila ★★★★☆ 29 Mar 2025 · ₱400–600 Bgy. 698 Malate, 1690-A Bocobo St, Malate, Manila, 1004 Metro Manila, Philippines One of the few remnants of old Malate, this cozy little pub still has its charm, with good grub, interesting patrons, and affordable drinks. They continue to serve cocktails by the pitcher, but now there’s also a selection of craft beers. The pulutan, like sisig and kinilaw, are reliably tasty. 2025 update: Half of the cocktail pitchers are out of stock, including my favorite mango daiquiri (sigh), but I did enjoy both the nachos and the tuna sisig. Prices are definitely creeping up, though—inflation is hitting hard
